 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal Year 2020 Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Company Delivers Results at High End of Guidance Range; Expects EPS Growth in Fiscal 2021 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fourth quarter Walgreens Boots Alliance highlights, year-over-year </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Sales increased 2.3&nbsp;percent to $34.7&nbsp;billion, up 2.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Operating income decreased 26.0&nbsp;percent to $650&nbsp;million; Adjusted operating income decreased
27.7&nbsp;percent to $1.1&nbsp;billion, down 27.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">EPS decreased 42.8&nbsp;percent to $0.43; Adjusted EPS decreased 28.2&nbsp;percent to $1.02, down
27.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis; reflecting an estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of approximately $0.46 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2020 highlights, year-over-year </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Sales increased 2.0&nbsp;percent to $139.5&nbsp;billion, up 2.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Operating income decreased 73.7&nbsp;percent to $1.3&nbsp;billion; Adjusted operating income decreased
24.9&nbsp;percent to $5.2&nbsp;billion, down 24.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">EPS decreased 88.0&nbsp;percent to $0.52; Adjusted EPS decreased 20.8&nbsp;percent to $4.74, down
20.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis; reflecting an estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of approximately $1.06 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net cash provided by operating activities was $5.5&nbsp;billion, a decrease of $109&nbsp;million compared with
fiscal 2019; Free cash flow increased 5.6&nbsp;percent to $4.1&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2021 guidance </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company introduced fiscal 2021 guidance of low single-digit growth in adjusted EPS at constant currency rates
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill., October&nbsp;15,&nbsp;2020 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the
fiscal year and fourth quarter that ended August&nbsp;31, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Executive Vice Chairman and CEO Stefano Pessina said, &#147;I am pleased to report
results that came in at the high end of our expectations as we continue to adapt and transform our business model to changing customer needs. Despite uncertainty amid the global <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, we are
seeing gradual improvement in key U.S. and UK markets and continued strong performance in our wholesale business. I&#146;m also encouraged by the accelerating growth in our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> platforms. Now, more than
ever, our pharmacy-centered business is at the heart of community healthcare and we are expanding on that role for the future. I continue to be inspired by the tireless efforts of our teams as they support and care for our customers, patients and
communities, while accelerating progress on our clear set of strategic priorities. Looking ahead, we are projecting adjusted EPS growth in fiscal 2021, as reflected in our new guidance.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fourth Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2020 fourth
quarter net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance decreased 44.9&nbsp;percent to $373&nbsp;million compared with the same quarter a year ago and net earnings per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> decreased
42.8&nbsp;percent to $0.43. Adjusted net earnings<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased 30.9&nbsp;percent to $887&nbsp;million, down 30.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Adjusted earnings per share were $1.02,
down 28.2&nbsp;percent on a reported currency basis and down 27.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The decreases in both net earnings and adjusted net earnings were primarily due to an estimated adverse <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of $0.46, lower U.S. pharmacy gross profit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus changes, partially offset by Transformational Cost
Management Program savings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the fourth quarter were $34.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of 2.3&nbsp;percent from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter on both a reported and constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income was $650&nbsp;million, a
decrease of 26.0&nbsp;percent from the same quarter a year ago. Adjusted operating income was $1.1&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 27.7&nbsp;percent from the same quarter a year ago, and a decrease of 27.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The
company estimates adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of approximately $520&nbsp;million, or 34 percentage points of growth. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $2.1&nbsp;billion in the fourth quarter, a decrease of $292&nbsp;million from the same quarter a year ago. Free
cash flow was $1.7&nbsp;billion, a decrease of $248&nbsp;million versus the same quarter last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal Year Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2020 net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance decreased 88.5&nbsp;percent to $456&nbsp;million, while net earnings per share<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> decreased 88.0&nbsp;percent to $0.52, compared with the prior year, primarily due to third quarter <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges and costs related to the
Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Excluding these items, adjusted net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> in fiscal 2020 decreased 24.5&nbsp;percent to $4.2&nbsp;billion, down 24.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the prior year. Adjusted earnings per share decreased
20.8&nbsp;percent to $4.74, down 20.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the prior year, primarily due to estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of approximately $1.06, lower U.S. pharmacy
gross profit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus changes, partially offset by Transformational Cost Management Program savings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales increased 2.0&nbsp;percent to $139.5&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2020 compared with the prior year. On a constant currency basis, sales increased
2.5&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in fiscal 2020 was $1.3&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 73.7&nbsp;percent from the prior year. Adjusted operating income
was $5.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 24.9&nbsp;percent, and a decrease of 24.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The company estimates adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of approximately $1.2&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $5.5&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2020, a decrease of $109&nbsp;million from fiscal 2019. Free cash flow was
$4.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of $219&nbsp;million from fiscal 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company today introduced fiscal 2021 guidance of low single-digit growth in adjusted earnings per share at constant currency rates. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">While the company anticipates a gradual reduction in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impacts, the first half results will continue to be
negatively impacted when compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-COVID-19</FONT></FONT> first half of fiscal 2020. However, for the second half, the company anticipates strong adjusted EPS growth, as
these effects subside and recovery plans take hold in key markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Significant investments in fiscal 2021 are expected to accelerate the company&#146;s
customer-centric approach, with specific focus on transforming omnichannel capabilities and offerings across retail and healthcare. These investments are expected to contribute to the second-half growth profile. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impacts, the evolution of the pandemic remains uncertain. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> could present both incremental risks as well as opportunities for the company&#146;s
business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Progress on Strategic Priorities </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Selected

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Expanding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> testing for businesses and preparing capability for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Divisions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail Pharmacy USA: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth quarter sales in Retail
Pharmacy USA increased 3.6&nbsp;percent to $27.0&nbsp;billion, including the impact of previously announced store closures, reflecting improved retail sales and prescription volume trends. Sales in comparable stores also increased 3.6&nbsp;percent
from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prescriptions filled in the fourth quarter increased 1.6&nbsp;percent compared with
the same quarter a year earlier. In comparable stores, prescriptions filled increased 3.6&nbsp;percent from a year earlier, an improvement of 3.2 percentage points compared with the third quarter. The number of prescriptions filled was
287.6&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. Pharmacy sales, which accounted for 75.6&nbsp;percent of the division&#146;s sales in the quarter, increased 4.2&nbsp;percent
compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 3.2&nbsp;percent. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The division&#146;s retail prescription market share on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
adjusted basis in the fourth quarter decreased approximately 30 basis points over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to 20.7&nbsp;percent, as reported by IQVIA. This result was mostly due to store closures. Retail
prescription market share in fiscal 2020 declined by 40 basis points to 20.9&nbsp;percent, compared with 21.3&nbsp;percent in fiscal 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales
increased 1.5&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, including the impact of store optimization programs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable retail sales increased 4.7&nbsp;percent, boosted by 15&nbsp;percent growth in the health and wellness category and 8&nbsp;percent growth in the
personal care category. This was partly offset by a 3&nbsp;percent decrease in the beauty category. Results were boosted by increased demand for PPE and by the performance of the mass personalization initiative. Walgreens.com sales grew
39&nbsp;percent in the quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 3.1&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, reflecting pharmacy reimbursement
pressure, lower retail margin due to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> mix impact and higher retail comprehensive loss. Adjusted gross profit decreased 4.5&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A decreased by 2.7&nbsp;percent, reflecting store optimization and acquisition related costs in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A decreased by 0.1&nbsp;percent as savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program offset <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related costs, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus changes, inflation and investments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the fourth quarter decreased
5.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $659&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating income in the fourth quarter decreased 22.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to
$884&nbsp;million. Operating income and adjusted operating income included an adverse impact of approximately $200&nbsp;million due to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail Pharmacy International: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail Pharmacy
International had fourth quarter sales of $2.3&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 14.9&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 0.5&nbsp;percent. Sales decreased
15.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly due to a 16.7&nbsp;percent decrease in Boots UK sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable retail sales decreased
29.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis as footfall in stores continued to be significantly reduced due to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> particularly in major high street, train station and airport locations. Footfall did,
however, improve steadily in the fourth quarter compared with the third quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK market share was lower in all categories except beauty, as the
pandemic continued to impact heavily on buying habits and consumers temporarily shifted purchasing to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-stop</FONT> grocery shopping. Boots.com sales growth accelerated to 155&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, partially offsetting the reduced footfall. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable pharmacy sales in Boots UK increased
0.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting favorable timing on National Health Service (NHS) reimbursement, which mitigated the impact of lower prescription volume and reduced demand for pharmacy services during the pandemic. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 24.7&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including a favorable currency impact of 0.7&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross
profit decreased 25.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower UK retail sales, higher fulfillment costs, marketing investments to drive customer traffic and lower fixed supplier contributions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A in the quarter decreased 8.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $964&nbsp;million, including an
adverse currency impact of 0.9&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, adjusted SG&amp;A decreased by 9.7&nbsp;percent. The decreases in SG&amp;A and adjusted SG&amp;A both reflect short-term cost mitigation initiatives and savings from the
Transformational Cost Management Program. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the fourth quarter decreased $181&nbsp;million from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to an operating loss of $132&nbsp;million, primarily as a result of retail sales in the UK. Adjusted operating income decreased $197&nbsp;million to an adjusted operating loss of
$3&nbsp;million. On a constant currency basis, adjusted operating income decreased $196&nbsp;million. The estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact on both operating income and adjusted operating income was
approximately $300&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Pharmaceutical Wholesale: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmaceutical Wholesale had fourth quarter sales of $6.0&nbsp;billion, an increase of 4.3&nbsp;percent from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. On a constant currency basis, sales increased 4.3&nbsp;percent, led by emerging markets, Germany and France. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the fourth quarter was $124&nbsp;million, which included $57&nbsp;million from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen,
compared with operating income of $129&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, which included $59&nbsp;million from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. Adjusted operating income increased
7.1&nbsp;percent to $245&nbsp;million, up 8.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly reflecting sales growth and cost management. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Dividends
Declared </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the fourth quarter the WBA board of directors declared a quarterly dividend of 46.75 cents per share, an increase of 2.2&nbsp;percent.
The dividend was payable September&nbsp;11, 2020 to stockholders of record as of August&nbsp;19, 2020, and raised the annual rate from $1.83 per share to $1.87 per share. This marked the 45th consecutive year that WBA and its predecessor company,
Walgreen Co., have raised the dividend, and the 87th year a dividend has been paid. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance will hold a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-hour</FONT> conference call to discuss the fourth quarter results beginning at 8:30
a.m. Eastern time today, October&nbsp;15, 2020. The conference call will be simulcast through the Walgreens Boots Alliance investor relations website at: <U>http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. A replay of the conference call will be
archived on the website for 12 months after the call. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The replay also will be available from 11:30 a.m. Eastern time, October&nbsp;15, 2020 through
October&nbsp;22, 2020 by calling +1 800 585 8367 within the U.S. and Canada, or +1 416 621 4642 outside the U.S. and Canada, using replay code 6490979. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> All references to earnings per share (EPS) are to diluted EPS attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">ENDS </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance
(Nasdaq: WBA) is a global leader in retail and wholesale pharmacy, touching millions of lives every day through dispensing and distributing medicines, and through its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. The
company has more than 100 years of trusted healthcare heritage and innovation in community pharmacy and pharmaceutical wholesaling. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Including equity
method investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 450,000 people and has more than 21,000 stores. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA&#146;s purpose is
to help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA is a Participant of the United Nations
Global Compact and adheres to its principles-based approach to responsible business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA is included in FORTUNE&#146;s 2020 list of the World&#146;s Most
Admired Companies*, ranked first in the food and drugstore category. This is the 27th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company, Walgreen Co., has been named to the list. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More company information is available at https://www.walgreensbootsalliance.com/. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures
calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not
calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s
financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such
constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding
the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The twelve months ended August&nbsp;31, 2020 comparable sales and prescriptions filled figures for the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions exclude the
benefit of this year&#146;s leap day. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions, comparable stores are defined as those that have been open for at
least 12 consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months. Relocated stores are not included as
comparable stores for the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable stores for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable store sales, comparable
pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions
and number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively, in such stores. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146;
methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the Retail Pharmacy International division, comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are
presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company considers certain
metrics, including all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s
management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period
to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures
presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>

proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in order
to provide investors with a comparable view of performance across periods. These adjustments include acquisition-related amortization and acquisition-related costs and were immaterial for periods prior to the quarter ended May&nbsp;31, 2019.
Although the company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the company has
direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method
investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other
contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
